## Diagram 1

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[convertMeasurementUnits] --> B{Normalize unit to STANDARD_UNIT}
    B --> C[Get measurement type]
    C --> D{measurement === undefined?}
    D -->|Yes| E[Return original unit & value]
    D -->|No| F[Get user preferences]
    F --> G[Get preferred unit from preferences]
    G --> H[Normalize preferred unit]
    H --> I[Convert value using convert library]
    I --> J{convertedValue exists?}
    J -->|Yes| K[Parse to float]
    K --> L{Has decimal places?}
    L -->|Yes| M[Format to 2 decimals]
    L -->|No| N[Keep as is]
    M --> O[Return preferredUnit & convertedValue]
    N --> O
    J -->|No| O
```

## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    A[User/App] --> B[setMeasurementUnits]
    B --> C[BrowserStorage]
    C --> D[getMeasurementUnitsFromUserPreferences]
    D --> E{Storage has value?}
    E -->|Yes| F[Parse & return stored units]
    E -->|No| G[Return DEFAULT_MEASUREMENT_UNIT]
    F --> H[User/App]
    G --> H
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class MeasurementUnitsModule {
        +getMeasurementUnitsFromUserPreferences()
        +setMeasurementUnits(unitsOfMeasurement)
        +convertMeasurementUnits(unit, value)
        -getMeasurementType(unit)
        -hasDecimalPlaces(num)
    }
    class DEFAULT_MEASUREMENT_UNIT {
        +String system
        +String mass
        +String pressure
        +String volume
        +String distance
        +String temperature
    }
    class STANDARD_UNIT {
        +String KPA
        +String PSI
        +String LB
        +String KG
        +String GAL
        +String L
        +String KM
        +String MI
        +String C
        +String F
    }
    class BrowserStorage {
        +String measurementUnit
    }
    MeasurementUnitsModule --> DEFAULT_MEASUREMENT_UNIT
    MeasurementUnitsModule --> STANDARD_UNIT
    MeasurementUnitsModule --> BrowserStorage
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant App
    participant Module
    participant Storage
    participant ConvertLib
    App->>Module: convertMeasurementUnits({unit, value})
    Module->>Module: Normalize unit with STANDARD_UNIT
    Module->>Module: getMeasurementType(unit)
    alt measurement type undefined
        Module->>App: Return original unit & value
    else measurement type found
        Module->>Storage: getMeasurementUnitsFromUserPreferences()
        Storage->>Module: User preferences or defaults
        Module->>Module: Get & normalize preferred unit
        Module->>ConvertLib: convert(value).from(unit).to(preferredUnit)
        ConvertLib->>Module: Converted value
        Module->>Module: hasDecimalPlaces(value)
        alt has decimals
            Module->>Module: Format to 2 decimals
        end
        Module->>App: Return preferredUnit & convertedValue
    end
```

## Diagram 5

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> CheckStorage: getMeasurementUnitsFromUserPreferences()
    CheckStorage --> StorageExists: Has stored value
    CheckStorage --> UseDefaults: No stored value
    StorageExists --> ParseJSON
    ParseJSON --> ReturnPreferences
    UseDefaults --> ReturnDefaults
    ReturnPreferences --> [*]
    ReturnDefaults --> [*]
    
    [*] --> ConversionStart: convertMeasurementUnits()
    ConversionStart --> NormalizeUnit
    NormalizeUnit --> GetMeasurementType
    GetMeasurementType --> InvalidType: undefined type
    GetMeasurementType --> ValidType: known type
    InvalidType --> ReturnOriginal
    ValidType --> FetchPreferences
    FetchPreferences --> ConvertValue
    ConvertValue --> CheckDecimals
    CheckDecimals --> FormatDecimals: Has decimals
    CheckDecimals --> ReturnConverted: No decimals
    FormatDecimals --> ReturnConverted
    ReturnOriginal --> [*]
    ReturnConverted --> [*]
```
